                         Located in one of the most famous bohemian area of São Paulo, the area can provide you a mix of cultural, leisure, gastronomic and healthy programs such as Ibirapuera Park, museums, cinemas, great restaurants and pubs for all tastes. Look the pics.

                        <div data-reactid="665">
                         On the 18th floor, it offers 1 bedroom (King size), 2 bathrooms, one big living room with easy access to the kitchen and laundry. The apartment is served by 3 big and comfortable elevators and 3 parking spaces. All domestic utensils and utilities are included in the rent. The building provides 24 hours surveillance. All windows have blinds and for the bedroom a blackout. 
                        </div>

                         The Ibirapuera neighborhood is one of the most trendy, visited and easy access in Sao Paulo. The Loft is located just a few blocks far from the great restaurants, supermarkets, bakeries, bars, drugstores, museums and the Ibirapuera Park. However, you can blast a good walk around and visit all these and many other places.

                         <li data-reactid="1066"><p data-reactid="1067">Wagner is a great host. He met me at the apartment and guided me through the check-in process. After that, he was largely hands off but quick to respond to a variety of needs I had -- new converters, options for late night ordering, the nearest DHL store, etc. The apartment is lovely. It is very clean and orderly and true to the pictures. It is missing a trash can in the kitchen. There are only wastebaskets throughout the house. But trash can be taken down stairs to the receptacles. Because I visited in Brazil's winter, it was chilly. I never figured out how to work the heat in the living room, but there is a nice large blanket, so this was not a problem. A few things I would have liked to have known ahead of time: Keep in mind that the shower and bathroom floor drains close. I almost flooded the apartment because I didn't realize this! Thankfully I did not and was able to wash in the unit the towels I used to clean up the mess I made. Also, you must lock the door with the key when you're inside. It does not lock on its own. The building staff is nice and the three-door system/fingerprint keypad feels secure. The area is generally quiet and there are guards outside at almost every apartment complex in the block. I am a petite woman that was staying alone, and I didn't feel unsafe at any point. Uber was also very easy to use in this area and to get around.                         <div data-reactid="1173">
                         Apartment next to the most beloved park of São Paulo. Puts up up to six people comfortably and with privacy. Has a large living room and kitchen equipped for all meals. Vila Mariana is a safe neighborhood, full of cultural attractions, bars and restaurants (walking distance). It is a few blocks from Ana Rosa subway Station, with access to green and blue lines. You will stay close to Downtown and Paulista, but in the tranquility of a residential neighborhood. Taxis and bicycles are easily found.

                        <div data-reactid="1174">
                         Facing the inner part of the block, this appartment is filled with tranquility. Confortable beds (with pocket springs mattress) you help you regain energy to start a fantastic new day in the city. There are doble beds in two rooms, and one a sofabed in the other. Several city guides will you help you plan your day, including the Ibirapuera park just a few meters away. The kitchen is also equipped with the basics for every day meals.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1175">
                         This central neighborhood offers easy access to two very interesting regions of the city: downtown and Paulista avenue. It is a safe neighborhood and filled with cultural and gastronomic attractions, all at walking distance from the apartment. Are you into sports or nature? Then you will love the proximity with Ibirapuera Park, the most famous park in the city and also elected one of the best parks in the world (The Guardian). The SESC Vila Mariana is just two blocks away and has a programming full of concerts, plays, besides activities for all ages. The Cinemateca Brasileira (a films cultural center) is also close by.
